<Text>I fell victim to the Deep Cleaning scam here also, I go to the dentist religiously and take care of my teeth. I just started going here because I moved far from my old dentist. It shocked me when they did my gum measurements, which was painful because it was pushed so deep to record astronomically high measurements. Never had I was nearly double my last measurements. They said I needed a deep clean, I was so shocked. I went ahead with it, then Francis said I needed to pay 50% of the cleaning which, I was not comfortable with. What kind of office takes money before the procedure when they are supposedly certain the patient would need the procedure. I was only comfortable paying half of it. So I paid half and my insurance and got the deep clean done. It was excruciatingly painful way more painful then I remember getting it done a decade ago. Anyways, my insurance covered it, because I've had a deep clean a decade ago.

Then I went on to read these reviews and it all makes sense now, they push the deep clean to everyone and roll the dice to see if the insurance would pay for it. This is why they collect money up front so you lock into doing the procedure. They rush you into doing the deep clean within the week so they don't have to file the preauthorization with the insurance company, because I called my insurance the day after the office said I needed a deep clean, all the office has to do is file a predetermination claim with the insurance. How does a dental office, not know this? they just want your money. I may or may not have needed a deep clean, but from the way they handle business and how I'm reading they treat other people the same way, I will not be going back here. If they suggest the deep clean, get a 2nd opinion, Shady business.<//Text>< pics>

<Rating>5< /Rating><pictures>None</pictures>< Text>
Back in August we brought in our Nissan Murano to FCC.  The involved repair job took 3 weeks and the service was seamless and smooth.  That's very important during every car repair situation, as it's always stressful for car owners.

We had an incident where our car incurred some body damage.  Nissan Sunnyvale referred us to FCC, so the tow truck driver took us here.

After we called our insurance State Farm, they told us that the other 2 FCC locations were on their certified body shop list, but this FCC was not (yet).  This location is their newest shop.   Even though they are not State Farm certified, State Farm could cover if the shop quotes and meets the insurance adjuster's estimate.

Throughout the whole process, FCC kept us informed of the State Farm quote process, and were able to keep the repairs within the State Farm estimate, even with a couple of minor adjustments for additional required work throughout the job.

At the end everything was fixed smoothly, with very smooth service from State Farm as well without any issues incurred on our side.

Danny at FCC was very helpful from FCC and made the experience very calm and the estimates very clear so everything was understood, and all payments were clear between State Farm, FCC, and us.

A great experience for us, even though you never look forward to going to an auto body shop.</Text>

< Text>
We needed a fender repair on our Nissan Leaf. Our previous experience with body shops had been poor to mediocre. After phone calls to Mercury Insurance and Nissan and quite a bit of Googling, I decided to call FCC on Arquez. It is family-owned, Arquez was convenient, and Nissan recommended them. Also, FCC had the fewest poor Yelp ratings online, although I do take those with a grain of salt.
I called on a Friday and Sheldon walked me through the entire process on the phone. I made an appointment for Monday am and called Mercury. Although FCC is not on their "list," Mercury coordinated with them right away.
When I showed up Monday, the office was clean and bright and they had already started a folder for me. Sheldon walked me through the paperwork. He and Danny are very polite and professional.
It took about two weeks to get my car fixed because they had to wait over a week for a part from Nissan. FCC had it ready to go after just a few days and coordinated with Mercury to extend the car rental.
When I picked up the car, it looked great and was clean inside and out. Sheldon said to contact him if anything shows up in the next few weeks.
All in all, a very positive experience. FCC is now my body shop of choice. And, this is fhe first review I have ever written for any good or service.</Text>

<GmapID>0x808fa315cb4239f3:0x768a243a70ddb824< /GmapID><user_id>106940451574897927130</user_id>< text>
We went to a Copa America game at Levi Stadium and it was after 10 p.m. on a Monday night. We stumbled on this place about 20 minutes away from the stadium and it appeared to be the only place open that late. We were surprised by the value and flavor of their tacos. All four of us ate at least 3 tacos each and had agua frescas for under $30. The carne asada tacos were good, but just be careful if you get "everything" on your tacos if you're sensitive to spicy salsa. This place was pretty popular considering it was a Monday night and there weren't any tables, but it was fun eating on the side of the window.</text>

It's a very nicely kept range. The covers portion is for 10 and 20 yards. The field section goes from 20 to 100. Range rules are pretty much the same as many others. No broadheaded arrows,  no crossbows,  5 minute windows before going down range. It is "recommended" that you bring target pads. Basically 3-5 layers of foam to protect the hay bales. People are very friendly and the area is nice.< /Review>

< Review>
Spacious park with plenty of parking, shade and entrances and exits pass/behind The Japanese Gardens.

There's lots of picnic tables and room to enjoy a day out with friends, family, etc.

The playground equipment seems to be in use but not sure who often it's treated or taken care of as far as cleaning, etc.

The area is very lush and green and they have a few bbq bits as well.

Some cool paths as well and trails to the Sepulveda Basin and natural wildlife.<//Review>

<review>This is a decent range with fita distances available and a covered range (lit at night!) to 18m. Archers all shoot from one line, which makes it much safer than many other public shooting spaces. There is officially a 5min time limit on ends, but shooting is untimed and unsupervised, so the actual pace of shooting varies widely. <pictures>None</pictures><text>We have been coming to this restaurant for at least 4 years. The food was good for the ‚Äúprice‚Äù and the service was great, very friendly staff.
We have been supporting them along with our other favorite restaurants all through Covid. Tonight we ordered our regular food; pot of tom Kai coconut soup, large white rice and an order of Paradise fried rice. The total was over $36. When we looked at the bill, the base price of the Paradise fried  rice went up from $11.95 to $15.95, an almost 35% increase (along with everything else, although they are still using the old menus so you don‚Äôt know how much the food is until you get the bill) I understand that times are difficult and restaurants have been especially hard hit with Covid so I could have accepted the price increase but then they also charged us $3.00 extra for the shrimp because unlike before at $11.95 that included both chicken and shrimp now it only includes one, to have both its extra. So in order for me to get the same dish as I had before at $11.95, it cost us $18.95, an increase of almost 60%!!! So not only did they increase their cost but they also give you less for more $$. I used to go to this restaurant very often since my daughter used to live close to it. Now she lives too far from it and I have been eating Thai food at other restaurants in the Lakewood/Long Beach area. On a day that I was in Downey, I decided to go back. I would say this is the reference I use whenever I rate Thai food. For me, this is still the best I have ever had. I'll definitely will go back if I'm in the Downey area.</Text>

<rate>5< /rate>< review>
The new owner, Dr. Murphy is amazing! My wife and I have been taking our pets to Dr. Murphy for over 10 years.  She is so good of a veterinarian, we followed her from her previous vet to her new practice here at Orange Canyon Pet Clinic. I feel bad that she inherited some of the issues from the previous owner/vet, but I'm confident all current and new clients will see how much love, care, and compassion she has for animals.

What makes Dr. Murphy so special is that she is a passionate vet. She doesn't rely on old practices alone, but rather continues to be aware of the latest in veterinary medicine and technology. For example, when our older cat, Mufasa, started having more difficulty with his irritable bowel disease (IBD), instead of adding more steroids, she switched him to a special diet and added a probiotic supplement. She explained to us that even though a higher dose of steroids may help address the IBD, it can lead to issues to the kidneys. And at his age (17 years old), the kidneys are already at risk. He has been doing fine since she adjusted his treatment. And his kidneys are doing fine as well.

Dr. Murphy has been with us and our pets through thick and thin. She was there for us when our other cat got cancer. She provided the best treatment and always took into consideration the financial aspect of the treatment. We knew, as did many of her other clients did, that she wasn‚Äôt going to leave any stone unturned, and she would work her hardest to provide the best treatment and care for our pets.

My wife and I have never met a vet that is as passionate, energetic, and knowledgeable as Dr. Murphy. We are thankful we found her years ago, and are happy she now runs her own practice.</review>

<Date>1409172790148</Date><Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
Dr. Black has doctored 8 of my dogs over the past 20 years. He was working with our original vet and we fell in love with him. We lost track of him for three years simply because he had left to start his own business and we simply lost touch.  As soon as I found him again, I immediately transferred my records to him.  Yes, his prices are higher but I have complete trust in his expertise and his talent. I could save money.  But I won't because my 20-year history has been superior. My dogs are my children and I insist on the best care.  His staff is the best.  Whenever I have checked in my dog I was given an itemized list of the costs.  This is the normal procedure.  This is the time the owner needs to tell them whether or not you would approve of the costs/procedures.  Once you sign the form, you are agreeing to the possibilities.  Frankly, I trust him so much that I've always told them to do what is necessary only.  Never have I felt over charged or was my dog over treated.  My dogs and I have always been treated like family.  I will stay with Dr. Black until I no longer have a dog.  And I plan on always having a dog.</review>

< review>
Great experience for my first visit.   Flavorful and inexpensive Mexican lunch buffet.  It's even cheaper than El Torito.  The food quality is good and tasty.  Options are limited but enough for you to choose from, and it will fill you up.  I came for their weekday lunch buffet 11am-2pm for $11.99.  Drinks are not included on the price.  Buffet includes menudo, caldo de albondigas, chile rellenos, rolled taquitos, chicken fajita, enchiladas, rice and beans, chile verde con carne, pork carnitas, salsa, pico de gallo, and much more.  Service staff are very helpful and friendly.  Plenty of parking.  I will definitely come back again.<//review>

<Date>1541489202267</Date><Rating>4</Rating><review>Today, I went to one of my favorite haunt's when I was passing thru Anaheim. I frequently revisit a restaurant/Deli that I enjoyed previously.
Today, my mood led me toward Margaritaville (maybe hearing it on the radio
had something to do with it...do you think?)

Damn subliminal messaging worked again!
Anyways, I sat at the bar and said to the bartender "I need a damn good tasting Margarita like I'm use to...he smiled and said that he can make it happen.

He brought me my Margarita and said to taste it because I came in at a good time.
After sipping it twice (I wanted to make sure before I spoke.)
I told him that it was a damn good tasting Margarita and will enjoy the rest once I decide on what to eat.

It was at this time, that he handed me a small bar menu which had several different "Happy Hour" food selections that all looked delicious.

After deciding on the Burrito with the chunks of pork which was marinated with a green sauce inside. I asked if it we're possible to make it "Wet with the red enchilada sauce"
He said no problem because it automatically is served that way.

Circling back to when he mentioned about coming in at a good time, he told me the wet burrito was $7.00 and the Margarita is only $4.00..such a deal.

I responded with a smile and said "that is incredible and let's get this show on the road.
It was about 10 min.that passed and he was already bringing out this large wet size burrito (with ez on the melting cheese.)

Let me tell you, that I enjoyed every last bite as I slathered some sour cream on top. I took a breather for about 5 min. and then finished off the second half with equal enjoyment.
I want to thank the bartender who worked the early afternoon shift for making my visit an enjoyable one. As usual, I'll be back.

<name>cmilton111< /name><review>Changed my rating from 2 to 4 stars.. We returned to Casa Gaming yesterday even though I had previously said I wasn't going to return.  This visit I gotta admit the food was very tasty. I ordered a soft Carnitas taco, enchilada on the dinner menu (there menu is extensive). My meal was very good. They serve chips before we ordered; the chips were thin, warm and the taste is excellent. The salsa is good; I add Pica de Gallo to add flavor to chips and my meal.

Before this recent visit I said:

The food was okay (about 3 stars). The interior is also 3 stars, exterior 2 stars.

Big problem with this restaurant (my visit) though, the margarita was terrible. Even worse than the terrible margarita was when I mentioned it to the manager he did nothing to make me a happy customer, not even offer to take it off my check. That reflects very poor management and showing me that he evidently doesn't care if I return. I had taken a small drink and asked the person I was with to taste it also. I asked him to look at the margarita, taste it, but he wouldn't do either. Both of us (his customers) agree it was very bad.

I was a bit persistent with the manager just how bad it was.."the worst margarita I have ever had", I told him. The waiter when asked about the drink told the manager with a shrug that it was a "Happy Hour" margarita...does that mean they serve bad margaritas during Happy Hour?

A side note on this is that one member of the family does like this restaurant and dines there fairly regularly; it reminds her of her family outings (but she drinks wine not the margaritas). She had warned me that the margaritas were bad.. I am sorry I didn't listen to her. I mean, how can you mess up a margarita? She said, "I love there food but I order a glass of wine, they can't ruin that).

In one other visit, I did like the Buffet.

I am not returning. Also, I can't recommend this restaurant with poor management because poor management is unacceptable.
